<p>I think it makes more sense to return an empty array</p>
<pre><code>// invalid input return null or throw an error
if (!setA || !setB) {
    return null;
}
if (!setA.length || !setB.length) {
    return []; 
}
// or do nothing since the for loop will not trigger anyway
</code></pre>

                <relative-time datetime="2016-05-23T18:33:30Z" class="no-wrap">May 23, 2016</relative-time>
              </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>Selection Sort, for example, makes the algorithm look extremely (impossibly) good at first glance - O(n) - because it's not showing the majority of the steps.</p>
<p>Instead of</p>
<pre><code>    for (var j = i + 1; j &lt; D.length; j++) {
        if (D[j] &lt; D[minJ]) {
            tracer._select(j);
            minJ = j;
            tracer._deselect(j);
        }
    }
</code></pre>
<p>it has to be more like</p>
<pre><code>    for (var j
</code></pre>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>Is there a reason why in <a href="https://github.com/keon/algorithms/blob/master/.travis.yml">travis CI config</a> the command <code>black --check . || true</code> is run? I don't see the point in checking if files needs to be reformatted if it's just going to be ignored anyways.</p>
<p>Currently running <code>black --line-length 127 --check .</code> -&gt; <code>399 files would be reformatted, 74 files would be left unchanged.</code></p>
<p>In additio</p>

              <a class="text-gray-dark" href="https://github.com/trekhleb/homemade-machine-learning/issues/17" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;explore.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;click_context&quot;:&quot;REPOSITORY_CARD&quot;,&quot;click_target&quot;:&quot;ISSUE&quot;,&quot;click_visual_representation&quot;:&quot;BIG_GOOD_FIRST_ISSUE&quot;,&quot;actor_id&quot;:60628828,&quot;record_id&quot;:427376689,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/topics/algorithm&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:60628828}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="f22ab900d3f46178d8d811d6071b775e5ab45c48b41442a09b0fed9fe3c1e8b5" data-ga-click="Explore, go to issue, location:good first issues;size:large;">
                theta[0] is caculated twice in per gradient_step at LinearRegression
</a>

            </h1>
          </div>

        </div>

        <div class="d-flex">
          <div class="mr-3">
            <img
              class="avatar avatar-user avatar-small"
              alt="alqbib"
              src="https://avatars1.githubusercontent.com/u/29174690?v=4"
              width="32"
              height="32"
            >
          </div>
          <div class="flex-auto" style="width: 80%;">
            <div class="Box Box--condensed position-relative timeline-comment--caret">
              <div class="Box-header f6 text-gray">
                <strong class="text-gray-dark text-bold">
                  alqbib
                </strong>

                  commented

                <relative-time datetime="2019-03-31T09:31:13Z" class="no-wrap">Mar 31, 2019</relative-time>
              </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <h1>Vectorized version of gradient descent.</h1>
<p>theta = theta * reg_param - alpha * (1 / num_examples) * (delta.T @ self.data).T</p>
<h1>We should NOT regularize the parameter theta_zero.</h1>
<p>theta[0] = theta[0] - alpha * (1 / num_examples) * (self.data[:, 0].T @ delta).T</p>
<p>the first code line ,theta include theta[0].<br>
so I think can write like this:<br>
theta[0] -= alpha * (1 / num_examples) * (self.data[:, 0].</p>

                  <div
                    class="position-absolute right-0 left-0 bottom-0 text-center"
                    style="background: linear-gradient(to top, rgba(255,255,255,1), rgba(255,255,255,0));"
                  >

                      Read more
</a>                  </div>
                </div>

            <div class="Box Box--condensed position-relative timeline-comment--caret">
              <div class="Box-header f6 text-gray">
                <strong class="text-gray-dark text-bold">
                  c1887
                </strong>

                  commented

                <relative-time datetime="2020-02-20T10:03:10Z" class="no-wrap">Feb 20, 2020</relative-time>
              </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p><strong>Chapter number or note title:</strong> Chapter 0, Exercise 2, Footnote 24</p>
<p><strong>Page number:</strong> 17</p>
<p><strong>Error description:</strong> The footnote says "Ja, das ist <em>das</em> [...]maschine". However, the German language has 3 different articles (der, die das). In this particular case, you want "die" instead of "das" [...]maschine.</p>
<p><strong>Suggested fix (if any):</strong><br>
Ja, das ist <em>die</em> Subatomar[...]maschine.</p>

                  <p>Hey <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/mgechev/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/mgechev">@mgechev</a>,<br>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p><strong>A more consistent  and multi-functional global level of verbosity control</strong>,<br>
suggest an enhancement  that will see  <code>print(...)</code>  in project be converted to using the python logging. module</p>
<pre><code>import logging
#Then instead of print() use either
logging.info(......)
#or
logging.debug(.....)
#or
logging.warning(....)
#or
#logging.error()
</code></pre>
<p>In that way verbosity  can be globally</p>
